I got the Thai hot pot this time and it was really good! The soup was flavorful, it had lots of veggies, toppings, and 2 large shrimps. It came with bun.

My friend got the bun bo hue bowl and she really enjoyed it. I thought it was a bit small, but she said it was perfect. She wanted it a little spicier, so she asked for the red chili on the side.

As usual, we had to end it with the Saigon sweetheart. Everyone loved it!</text>

Came here on a Saturday night around 7pm. When we walked in, the place wasn't packed, but it still took 15 min to get a table. We did get water right away. They only had 1 waiter and we had to wait about 20 min to get our food order taken. Anything I asked for, like drinks they didn't have, dessert as well.

Each plate of food came 5 to 10 min after each other. I ordered the seafood hot Pot and it came with more veggies than seafood. It also didn't have any taste. I also ordered the lemon wings and those did taste good.< /Text>

We came on a Wednesday at 1pm. The place wasn't busy, there were only 2 occupied tables when we came. The place was very spacious, loved the earthly tone of the furnitures and the decors. And since the place is almost empty, we got our orders real fast. The foods were delicious, the serving size was good. I can't compare how this place looks like when it's packed, but I'm glad we came on a non-peak hour. Service was very good too, not excellent but better than most. Overall, it was an enjoyable lunch for me and my son.<//text>

< Review>
This is my husband's and my favorite spot for dinner.  I really love hot pot, and Sizzle Spot's curry chicken pot is probably my favorite hot pot around.   The udon noodles are always cooked just right (not overcooked) and the veggies are crisp and cook just to your liking at the table.  I love the addition of the taro chunks to the coconut curry base.  So good!  My husband always gets the garlic steak sizzle plate -- definitely go for the butter bomb, because that just puts it over the top!  Sizzle Spot's boba tea offerings are delicious, too.  The atmosphere of the place is nice enough for a romantic dinner, but the price says "drop in anytime!"  Whenever we can't decide where to go for dinner, we always end up coming back to Sizzle Spot.< /Review>

<rate>4</rate>< review>
Awesome experience!! If you like Pepper Lunch(Milpitas) you will love this place more or if you haven't you will not regret.

Bigger portions and tastes better. If you like crispy edge burnt rice/noodles this place does it just right on your sizzling plate. You are able to customize dish with rice/noodles, meat, and veggies. Don't be fooled by picture...you get alot probably from 1 sizzling dish without the extra meat. It also comes with a side pickled cabbage similar that goes well when mixing with your main dish. Cup of water doesn't taste like faucet water like other Asian food places.

Online reservation elimates long waiting time. Why wait when you can spend the other time doing other things you want. Also the space is decent size so no worrying about being in crammed up space and hot plates hitting your face.

My only criticism would be that the tables/chair could use a bit of wipe down.

Highly recommend this place for group lunch or dinner!</review>

We popped in here on a nice Sunday evening, ready to get some sweet sizzle pan dindin, and we were very pleased with our meal!  It was quite funny: the meals were pretty big, so we asked for a box to go, but the owner must have thought that we didn't like the food, because she seemed quite distraught by our request.

THE FOOD WAS AMAZING!! AND WE WILL BE BACK!

I wouldn't say the serving sizes are mind-blowingly large, but they are very generous.  Especially if you are a little guy, which I am not, but if you are, then I'm sure you will find that you are adequately served.  Also got one of the coconut drinks, and it was amaze-ballz, but I am a huge fan of coconut, so I probably wouldn't be the person to ask how good it really was.  I loved it though.

One thing you should probably watch out for, this being in an Asian plaza, is the parking can get insanely crowded, so just make sure you come prepared for some hassle if you can't avoid it.</Text>

<Review>I'm always on the hunt for new boba and/or pastry places. Somehow I stumbled across Cali Bakehouse on Yelp and the pretty pictures of its interior intrigued me enough to convince me to pay them a visit. While I expected the cafe to be much more crowded based on its reviews and the pastry selection a bit more extensive.. I was not disappointed by my two visits this past weekend.

TEA -- We got their honey roasted oolong milk tea because we like the roasted flavor. This drink really hit the spot, but they need to work on consistency. This is not necessarily a negative though, because they were happy to add more tea for that kick of tea flavor when I thought my milk tea was too milky. The popping boba add-on in different flavors is a subtle and fun way to add extra flavor to your drink.

FOOD/PASTRIES -- To be honest, from the pictures, somehow I thought they had a bigger selection. I wasn't disappointed, but I wish they would heat up the pastries for you if you chose to dine-in. Again, some issues with consistency here.. On both visits we opted for Almond filled croissants.. Visit #1 the croissant LOOKED perfect but tasted stale. Visit #2 the  croissant lacked any almonds on top of it but tasted a bit fresher. These aren't a huge deal, but I feel like consistency would help improve the experience. They also offer miscellaneous sandwiches, and small bites for those hungering for more.

SERVICE -- really friendly, warm service. They actually SMILE. Twice in one visit, I was asked by two different people whether everything was good and if I needed them to adjust my drink in any way. I asked them to add more tea in my drink during my second visit and felt awful about it... But they didn't seem to resent me, whew.

INTERIOR/AMBIANCE -- whoever decorated this place should come decorate my house... Huge floor to ceiling windows allow SO MUCH natural light into the bakery, the pastries are located in a centerpiece of sorts directly in front of the door. The plates you use to hold your pastry picks are adorable. The seating includes these nice, huge, plush-like couches placed around the cafe. Lots of plants and small detail decorations add an extra flair to each table.

Cali Bakehouse definitely has a spot on my list for when I crave boba/pastries. Will be back!!<//Review>< Response>
None< /Response>

I've personally had over 7-8 screens replaced here, with an average of 100$ a screen lets just say I've done plenty of business with them. But today, 12/1/17 I walk in and I'm met by two faces I've never seen before. I tell them I just want the 80$ screen replacement. He spends the next 5 minutes trying to sell me a 200+$ " protection plan " for a phone that's not even worth 200$ anymore. After I've made it clear I just want a screen, he says give them about an hour,(even though the sign outside says *30 MINUTE FAST REPAIRS*) and when I return he claimed I need a battery because the battery was creating heat. He tried to sell me a battery for 50$ + tax then he tried selling me the " protection plan " saying i can save money and spend like 170 if I got the battery now. I declined all this because my battery was working fine before. So then I return because now the sim card is not being read by the iphone. When I return, he instantly goes in the back to whisper with his colleague, and comes back and instantly says " well we don't touch the sim card tray at all, but we will check out". After another half an hour, the guy comes out and says " so you see the sim card here ? It appears it's getting hot, it must be internal. " After he JUST TOLD ME the battery was getting hot..... I asked if they could honor a refund or discount of any sort being I just fixed a phone for nothing if it wasn't gonna work anymore to which he instantly said no, with no apologies or anything. Moral of my review ? This place has completely changed from fixing phone screens to trying to take your money by offering all this extra garbage and if you have even the slightest issue, they will basically tell you it's not their fault and gladly keep your money. Even if you're a 4+ year loyal customer. I will NEVER come here again and will advise all my friends not to as well. SMARTPHONE SCAM is what I will call them from now on.

The rental process was decent, I think there was another individual working there who was helping another person move the fridge? But no point were taken off because of that, I don't think he had another computer or terminal to help me even if he wanted to. But, when lines got long at Enterprise, I do recall where an agent would walk me out with a couple of keys and inform me which car I would like to rent instead of having me just wait in a long line and to start the paperwork. The selection of the vehicle were limited to 1 of each of the category. I had put a hold on an intermediate which happened to be a Hyundai Elantra, when I did the walk around, it looks like it had been in a slight fender bender and the rear bumper was sticking out a little bit on the right rear wheel well. Yes just a little bit, but I did not the bumper to strip off while I was driving down the Highway at a constant speed for 5 hours plus. It has happened before so I informed them this vehicle is deemed hazardous so I will not accept this, maybe a little eye roll was given to me ... but safety is an issue to my family and I.

I was then given another alternative, which I am sure would have been the same price for a smaller size which is compact even though I paid for the upgrade for midsize which was for a Scion XA in which, I know I am unable to put my pregnant wife and a car seat for my child to sit comfortably.

To which I asked do you have any other vehicles, she said let me go back in and check, mind you the parking lot is very small. If you don't know the inventory of what seemed like 3-4 cars in the lot was a bit frustrating. So we go back and she said, we have a Toyota Camry, I said fine we will take that. In my mind, a free upgrade would be nice because the other vehicle didn't seem safe. She said it was going to be $15 more. I said can you make it $10, she said no at first, then asked her co-worker to which she obliged. I just didn't know it was going to be $10 a day.

In my mind Sonata, Elantra vs. Toyota Camry, same thing, didn't I reserve a Midsize, not a compact. I thought they could have handled this issue more professionally when I told them the car was unsafe. I asked about the oil and maintenance, tire pressure, etc and received a response of they get maintenance to their respective mileage, fair enough, I wanted to check the oil level but I don't think she was having it. So I rented the car the car runs great, funny thing was on my trip back home, the Maintenance light came on for a brand new Toyota Camry at 4689 miles or something.
